   <div class="article-title-box">
    <h1 class="title-article" id="articleContentId">
     文本对抗样本系列的论文阅读笔记（整理合订）
    </h1>
   </div>
  </div>
 </div>
 <article class="baidu_pl">
  <div class="article_content clearfix" id="article_content">
   <link href="./../assets/css/kdoc_html_views-1a98987dfd.css" rel="stylesheet"/>
   <link href="./../assets/css/ck_htmledit_views-704d5b9767.css" rel="stylesheet"/>
   <div class="markdown_views prism-atom-one-dark" id="content_views">
    <svg style="display: none;" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
     <path d="M5,0 0,2.5 5,5z" id="raphael-marker-block" stroke-linecap="round" style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">
     </path>
    </svg>
    <h2>
     <a id="_0">
     </a>
     文本对抗样本系列的论文阅读笔记
    </h2>
    <p>
     以前调研文本对抗样本时的论文笔记梳理，论文都很经典，有现成的框架（TextAttack）可以直接用，论文中部分内容直接是截取自论文，所以存在中英混合笔记的情况。
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="BERTAttack_2">
     </a>
     BERT-Attack
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      作者：Linyang Li, Ruotian Ma, et al.
     </p>
     <p>
      单位：复旦大学
     </p>
     <p>
      来源：EMNLP 2020
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="Introduction_10">
     </a>
     Introduction
    </h4>
    <p>
     对抗样本：imperceptible to human judges while they can mislead the neural networks to incorrect predictions.
    </p>
    <p>
     文本对抗样本与图像对抗样本的区别：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       imperceptible to human judges &amp; misleading to models
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       fluent in grammar and semantically consistent with original inputs
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     先前的工作特点：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       based on specific rules
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       difficult to guarantee the fluency and semantically preservation in the generated adversarial samples at the same time.
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       rather complicated
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     核心思想：将BERT当作对抗样本的生成器，生成对抗样本
    </p>
    <p>
     BERT-Attack的优势：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       Training -&gt; Semantic-preserving
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Context around -&gt; fluent &amp; reasonable
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       inference the language model once as a perturbation generator rather than repeatedly using language models to score the generated adversarial samples in a trial and error process
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     实验效果：successfully fooled the downstream models
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="Related_Work_40">
     </a>
     Related Work
    </h4>
    <p>
     character-level heuristic rules: Jin et al. 2019
    </p>
    <p>
     substituting words with synonyms: Ren et.al 2019, Li et al. 2018
    </p>
    <p>
     score perturbations by searching for close meaning words in the embedding space: Alzantot et al. 2018
    </p>
    <p>
     semantically enhanced embedding but context unaware: Jin et al. 2019
    </p>
    <p>
     replace words manually to break the language inference system: Glockner et al. 2018
    </p>
    <p>
     replacement strategies using embedding transition: Lei et al. 2019
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="Method_54">
     </a>
     Method
    </h4>
    <p>
     两个步骤：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       finding the vulnerable words of target model
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       replacing the vulnerable words with semantically similar and grammatically correct words until a successful attack
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h5>
     <a id="Finding_Vulnerable_Words_62">
     </a>
     Finding Vulnerable Words
    </h5>
    <p>
     输入序列：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        S 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         [ 
        
        
        
          w 
         
        
          0 
         
        
       
         , 
        
       
         ⋯ 
         
       
         , 
        
        
        
          w 
         
        
          i 
         
        
       
         , 
        
       
         ⋯

    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">

         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ：目标模型正确标签的logit输出
    </p>
    <p>
     重要性分数：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        I 
         
         
         
           w 
          
         
           i 
          
         
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          o

         ( 
        
       
         S

          S 
         
         
         
           / 
          
          
          
            w 
           
          
            i

           1 
          
         
        
       
         , 
        
       
         ⋯ 
         
       
         ] 
        
       
      
        S_{/w_i}=[w_0,\cdots,w_{i-1},[MASK],w_{i+1},\cdots]

             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="minner">
          ⋯
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
           w
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mbin mtight">
                  −
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  1
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2083em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          [
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">
          M
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          S
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
          K
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          ]
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
           w
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mbin mtight">

                 </span>

           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">

         <span class="minner">
          ⋯
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          ]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     将评分排序，创造单词列表
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        L 
        
       
      
        L
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          L
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，取前
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        ϵ 
        
       
      
        \epsilon
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          ϵ
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     分数的单词作为攻击单词目标
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="Word_Replacement_via_BERT_72">
     </a>
     Word Replacement via BERT
    </h5>
    <p>
     Previous approaches: 多个人工规则，例如Synonym dictionary(Ren et al. 2019)、POS Checker(Jin et al. 2019)，Semantic Similarity Checker(Jin et al. 2019)
    </p>
    <p>
     这些替代策略缺陷：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       unaware of the context between the substitution position
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       insufficient in fluency control and semantic consistency
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     使用BERT进行替代策略解决fluency control与semantic preservation的问题：
    </p>
    <p>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/7a829c60c59040cfb0fc15bcfa3c2c0b.png"/>
    </p>
    <p>
     算法流程：
    </p>
    <p>
     <img alt="外链图片转存失败,源站可能有防盗链机制,建议将图片保存下来直接上传" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/ffd78380c4bb4fad94de512a880fdf8e.png"/>
    </p>
    <p>
     BPE算法将
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        S 
        
       
      
        S
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          S
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     进一步分词为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        H 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         [ 
        
        
        
          h 
         
        
          0 
         
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          h 
         
        
          1 
         
        
       
         , 
        
       
         ⋯ 
         
       
         ] 
        
       
      
        H=[h_0,h_1,\cdots]
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0813em;">
          H
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          [
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           h
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 0
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           h
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 1
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="minner">
          ⋯
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          ]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，因此需要进行分词对齐
    </p>
    <p>
     令
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        M 
        
       
      
        M
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">
          M
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     表示为BERT模型，则输出结果为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        P 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         M 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         H 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        P=M(H)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
          P
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">
          M
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0813em;">
          H
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     。在每个位置上使用最可能的
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        K 
        
       
      
        K
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
          K
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     词预测，
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        K 
        
       
      
        K
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
          K
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     是超参数。遍历预测的
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        K 
        
       
      
        K
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
          K
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     个词，得到对抗样本
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      单一词
     </strong>
     ：对于单词
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        w 
         
        
          j 
         
        
       
      
        w_j
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7167em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
           w
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                 j
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，其top-
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        K 
        
       
      
        K
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
          K
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     个预测候选为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        P 
         
        
          j 
         
        
       
      
        P^j
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8247em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
           P
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8247em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                 j
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     。通过NLTK过滤停止词，使用synonym dictionaries过滤反义词。最终构建干扰序列
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        H 
         
        
          ′ 
         
        
       
         = 
        
       
         [ 
        
        
        
          h 
         
        
          0 
         
        
       
         , 
        
       
         ⋯ 
         
       
         , 
        
        
        
          h 
         
         
         
           j 
          
         
           − 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          c 
         
        
          k 
         
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          h 
         
         
         
           j 
          
         
           + 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
         , 
        
       
         ⋯ 
         
       
         ] 
        
       
      
        H'=[h_0,\cdots, h_{j-1},c_k,h_{j+1},\cdots]
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7519em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0813em;">
           H
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7519em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  ′
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0361em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          [
         </span>

               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                 <span class="mbin mtight">
                  +
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  1
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="minner">
          ⋯
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          ]
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，如果能成功逆转结果，则该序列为对抗样本
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        H 
         
         
         
           a 
          
         
           d 
          
         
           v 
          
         
        
       
      
        H^{adv}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8491em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0813em;">
           H
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8491em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  a
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  d
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                  v
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     。否则，在
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        L 
        
       
      
        L
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          L
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     中查找下一个单词继续挑选最佳干扰项
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      分词
     </strong>
     ：perplexity指标寻找合适的单词替代。给定单词
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        w 
        
       
      
        w
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
          w
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的分词串
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        [ 
        
        
        
          h 
         
        
          0 
         
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          h 
         
        
          1 
         
        
       
         , 
        
       
         ⋯ 
         
       
         , 
        
        
        
          h 
         
        
          t 
         
        
       
         ] 
        
       
      
        [h_0,h_1,\cdots,h_t]
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          [
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           h
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 0
                </span>

         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">

         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           h
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">

         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           h
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">

              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

     ，根据
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        M

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">

     </span>
     列出来自预测
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        P 
         
         
         
           t 
          
         
           × 
          
         
           K 
          
         
        
       
      
        P^{t\times K}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8413em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
           P
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">

            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的所有可能组合，从而通过逆转BERT分词过程以转换这些二分词到正常单词之中
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="_101">
     </a>
     实验
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      数据集
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <p>
       Text Classification
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <p>
         Yelp: review classification dataset
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p>
         IMDB: document-level movie review dataset
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p>
         AG’s News: sentence-level news-type classification dataset
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p>
         FAKE: fake news classification dataset
        </p>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Natural Language Inference
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <p>
         SNLIL: Stanford language INFERENCE TASK
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p>
         MNLI: language inference dataset on multi-genre texts
        </p>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      Baseline
     </strong>
     : TextFooler, GA
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      Evaluation
     </strong>
     :
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       Attacked Accuracy
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Perturb Percentage
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Query Number
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Average Length
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Semantic Similarity (Universal Sentence Encoder)
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>

    <h3>
     <a id="Semantically_Equivalent_Adversarial_Rules_for_Debugging_NLP_Models_157">
     </a>
     Semantically Equivalent Adversarial Rules for Debugging NLP Models
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      作者：Marco Tulio Ribeiro, Sameer Singh et al.
     </p>
     <p>
      单位：University of Washington, University of California (Irvine)
     </p>
     <p>
      来源：ACL 2018
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="Introduction_166">
     </a>
     Introduction
    </h4>
    <p>
     Challenges:
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       different ways of phrasing the same sentence can often cause the model to output different predictions.
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       oversensitivity
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     提出的对抗样本方法：SEA
     <br/>
     优势：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       model-agnostic
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       generate semantically equivalent rules for optimal rule sets: semantic equivalence, high adversary count, non-redundancy.
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h4>
     <a id="Semantically_Equivalent_Adversaries_181">
     </a>
     Semantically Equivalent Adversaries
    </h4>
    <p>
     给定黑盒模型
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        f 
        
       
      
        f
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
          f
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，句子
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
        
       
      
        x
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，预测结果为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        f 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        f(x)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
          f
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     基本思想：通过调整
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
        
       
      
        x
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，以改变
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        f 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        f(x)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
          f
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     指示函数：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        S 
        
       
         e 
        
       
         m 
        
       
         E 
        
       
         q 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          ′ 
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         I 
        
       
         [ 
        
       
         S 
        
       
         e 
        
       
         m 
        
       
         E 
        
       
         q 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          ′ 
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         ∧ 
        
       
         f 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         ≠ 
        
       
         f 
        
       
         ( 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          ′ 
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         ] 
        
       
      
        SemEq(x,x')=\mathbb{I}[SemEq(x,x')\wedge f(x)\not=f(x')]
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0019em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          S
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          e
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          m
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
          Eq
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7519em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  ′
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0019em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathbb">
          I
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          [
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          S
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          e
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          m
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
          Eq
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7519em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  ′
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          ∧
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
          f
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          <span class="mord vbox">
           <span class="thinbox">
            <span class="rlap">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
             </span>
             <span class="inner">
              <span class="mord">
               <span class="mrel">
                
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="fix">
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>

    <h4>
     <a id="Semantically_Equivalent_Adversarial_Rules_SEARs_197">
     </a>
     Semantically Equivalent Adversarial Rules (SEARs)
    </h4>
    <p>
     假设：人的时间受限，愿意看
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        B 
        
       
      
        B
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
          B
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     条规则
    </p>
    <p>
     SEARs：给定一个参考数据集
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        X 
        
       
      
        X
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
          X
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，根据
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        X 
        
       
      
        X
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
          X
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     选择规则集
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        B 
        
       
      
        B
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
          B
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     规则形式：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        r 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         a 
        
       
         → 
        
       
         c 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        r=(a\rightarrow c)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
          r
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          a
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          →
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        a 
        
       
      
        a
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          a
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     为原始单词，
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        c 
        
       
      
        c
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     为替代词
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      构建规则集
     </strong>
     ：提取匹配词对，挑选最小连续序列使得
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
        
       
         → 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          ′ 
         
        
       
      
        x\rightarrow x'
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          →
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7519em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7519em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  ′
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     。同时包含中间上下文， e.g. What color
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        → 
        
       
      
        \rightarrow
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.3669em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          →
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     Which color。通过粗粒度和细粒度的Part-of-Speech tags乘积泛化，如果tags能匹配上前项，则允许这些tags出现在结果之中，e.g. What NOUN
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        → 
        
       
      
        \rightarrow
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.3669em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          →
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     Which NOUN
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      选择规则集
     </strong>
     ：给定候选规则，想要挑选规则集
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        R 
        
       
      
        R
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0077em;">
          R
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     使得
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        ∣ 
        
       
         R 
        
       
         ∣ 
        
       
         ≤ 
        
       
         B 
        
       
      
        |R|\leq B
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          ∣
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0077em;">
          R
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          ∣
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          ≤
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
          B
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <p>
       语义相等：在集合中规则的应用应该产生语义相等的实例，即：
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          E 
          
         
           [ 
          
         
           S 
          
         
           e 
          
         
           m 
          
         
           E 
          
         
           q 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           r 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ] 
          
         
           ≥ 
          
         
           1 
          
         
           − 
          
         
           δ 
          
         
        
          E[SemEq(x,r(x))]\geq 1-\delta
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
            E
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            [
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
            S
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            e
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            m
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
            Eq
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            x
           </span>
           <span class="mpunct">
            ,
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
            r
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            x
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            ))]
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            ≥
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            1
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mbin">
            −
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0379em;">
            δ
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       （Filter操作）
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       高对抗样本数量：能在验证集中诱导尽可能多的SEAs，并且语义相似分数高
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       不重复：不同的规则可能造成相同的SEAs，或者诱导不同的SEAs到相同的实例上，即目标函数：
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          max 
            
           
             ⁡ 
            
           
           
           
             R 
            
           
             , 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             R 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             &lt; 
            
           
             B 
            
           
          
          
          
            ∑ 
           
           
           
             x 
            
           
             ∈ 
            
           
             X 
            
           
          
          
           
           
             max 
            
           
             ⁡ 
            
           
           
           
             r 
            
           
             ∈ 
            
           
             R 
            
           
          
         
           S 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           r 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           S 
          
         
           E 
          
         
           A 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           r 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          \max\limits_{R,|R|&lt;B}\sum\limits_{x\in X}\max\limits_{r\in R}S(x,r(x))SEA(x,r(x))
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.7717em; vertical-align: -1.0217em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mop op-limits">

    <h4>
     <a id="User_Studies_223">

     User Studies
    </h4>
    <p>
     neural machine translation models parameters: default OpeNMT-py parameters
    </p>
    <p>
     POS tagging: spacy library
    </p>
    <p>
     SEAR generation:
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        δ 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         0.1 
        
       
      
        \delta=0.1
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0379em;">
          δ
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          0.1
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ,
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">

         = 
        
       
         0.0008 
        
       
      
        \tau=0.0008
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1132em;">
          τ
         </span>

     VQA:
     <em>
      telling
     </em>
     system, questions include “What”, “Where”, “When”, “Who”, “Why”, and “How”.

    <p>
     <strong>
      专家 VS SEA
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <p>
     <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/7fe12a4e75a342de9e2113f49e808bab.png"/>
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="TextBugger_Generating_Adversarial_Text_Against_Realworld_Applications_247">
     </a>
     TextBugger: Generating Adversarial Text Against Real-world Applications
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      作者：Jingfeng Li, ShouJing Ji et al.
     </p>
     <p>
      单位：浙江大学计算机学院
     </p>
     <p>
      来源：NDSS 2019
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="Introduction_256">
     </a>
     Introduction
    </h4>
    <p>
     对抗攻击分类
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <p>
       causative attacks: manipulate the training data to mislead the classifiers
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       exploratory attacks: craft malicious testing instances to evade a given classifiers
      </p>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     文本对抗样本的挑战：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       discrete property, hard to optimize
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       small perturbations are usually clearly perceptible
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       replacement of a single word may drastically alter the semantics of the sentence
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     已有工作(2019年前)缺陷：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       not computationally efficient
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       under the white-box setting
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       manual intervention
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       against a particular NLP model, not comprehensively evaluated
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     本文提出的TextBugger，分为白盒跟黑盒情景：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <p>
       白盒：通过计算分类器的Jacobian矩阵找到关键词，然后通过生成五种扰动选择最优扰动放进去
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       黑盒：首先寻找重要句子，之后选择打分函数寻找句子中的重要单词污染语料
      </p>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h4>
     <a id="Attack_Design_288">
     </a>
     Attack Design
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="Problem_Formulation_290">
     </a>
     Problem Formulation
    </h5>
    <p>
     受害模型

    <h5>
     <a id="Threat_Model_298">
     </a>
     Threat Model
    </h5>
    <p>
     白盒设置：complete knowledge about the targeted model architecture parameters (worst-case attack)
    </p>
    <p>
     黑盒设置：users can only access the model via an API (not aware of the model architecture)
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="TextBugger_304">
     </a>
     TextBugger
    </h5>
    <p>
     白盒攻击：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       寻找重要单词：给定
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          x 
          
         
           = 
          
         
           (

            x 
           
          
            2 
           
          
         
           , 
          
         
           ⋯ 
           
         
           , 
          
          
          
            x 
           
          
            N 
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          x=(x_1,x_2,\cdots,x_N)
         </span>

       为第i个单词，目标模型为
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">

          J_F(x)=\frac{\partial F(x)}{\partial x}=[\frac{\partial F_j(x)}{\partial x_i}]_{i\in\{1,\cdots,N\},j\in \{1,\cdots,K\}}

                        <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                         <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                         </span>
                         <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                          <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                           i
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span class="vlist-s">
                        ​
                       </span>

                      <span class="vlist-r">
                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;">

                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="" style="top: -3.23em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">

                 <span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;">

                <span class="" style="top: -3.5073em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">

                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0556em;">
                    ∂
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
                     F
                    </span>
                    <span class="msupsub">
                     <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                      <span class="vlist-r">
                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1645em;">
                        <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                         <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                         </span>
                         <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                          <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                           y
                          </span>

                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span class="vlist-s">

                      <span class="vlist-r">
                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2819em;">

                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span class="mopen mtight">
                    (
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    x
                   </span>
                   <span class="mclose mtight">

                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>

              <span class="vlist-r">

             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="mclose nulldelimiter">

           </span>

         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Bugs生成：考虑字符级扰动和单词级扰动。
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <p>
         字符级：将重要单词转化为未知单词
        </p>
       </li>
       <li>
        <p>
         单词级：插入、删除、交换、替代字符、替代单词
        </p>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     白盒攻击下的算法：
    </p>

       ，逆序排列句子重要性分数，其句子的重要性分数表示为：

     <li>
      <p>
       找到重要单词：找到最重要单词，并通过控制语义相似进行修改。设计了一个新的打分函数：
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          C 
           
           
           
             w 
            
           
             j 
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
          
          
            F 
           
          
            y 
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            w 
           
          
            1 
           
          
         
           , 
          
          
          
            w 
           
          
            2 
           
          
         
           , 
          
         
           ⋯ 
           
         
           , 
          
          
          
            w 
           
          
            m 
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           − 
          
          
          
            F 
           
          
            y 
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            w 
           
          
            1 
           
          
         
           , 
          
         
           ⋯ 
           
         
           , 
          
          
          
            w 
           
           
           
             j 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
         
           , 
          
          
          
            w 
           
           
           
             j 
            
           
             + 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
         
           , 
          
         
           ⋯ 
           
         
           , 
          
          
          
            w 
           
          
            m 
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          C_{w_j}=F_y(w_1,w_2,\cdots,w_m)-F_y(w_1,\cdots,w_{j-1},w_{j+1},\cdots,w_m)
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0307em; vertical-align: -0.3473em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
             C
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0715em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
                     w
                    </span>
                    <span class="msupsub">
                     <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                      <span class="vlist-r">
                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3281em;">
                        <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                         <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                         </span>
                         <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                          <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                           j
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span class="vlist-s">
                        ​
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="vlist-r">
                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2819em;">
                        <span class="">
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3473em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            =
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0361em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
             F
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                   y
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">

    <h4>
     <a id="Attack_Evaluation_332">
     </a>
     Attack Evaluation
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="Sentiment_Analysis_334">
     </a>
     Sentiment Analysis
    </h5>
    <p>
     数据集：IMDB，Rotten Tomatoes Movie Reviews (MR)
    </p>
    <p>
     受害模型：LR，CNN，LSTM
    </p>
    <p>
     baseline: Random，FGSM+Nearest Neighbor Search (NNS)，DeepFool+NNS
    </p>
    <p>
     评估指标：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <p>
       Edit Distance
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Jaccard Similarity Coefficient:
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          J 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           A 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           B 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           = 
          
          
           
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             A 
            
           
             ∩ 
            
           
             B 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
           
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             A 
            
           
             ∪ 
            
           
             B 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
          
           
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             A 
            
           
             ∩ 
            
           
             B 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
           
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             A 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             + 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             B 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             A 
            
           
             ∩ 
            
           
             B 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
          
         
        
          J(A,B)=\frac{|A\cap B|}{|A\cup B|}=\frac{|A\cap B|}{|A|+|B|-|A\cap B|}
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0962em;">
            J
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            A
           </span>
           <span class="mpunct">
            ,
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
            B
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            =
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.53em; vertical-align: -0.52em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
            </span>
            <span class="mfrac">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.01em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.655em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    ∣
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    A
                   </span>
                   <span class="mbin mtight">
                    ∪
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
                    B
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    ∣
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="" style="top: -3.23em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;">
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="" style="top: -3.485em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    ∣
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    A
                   </span>
                   <span class="mbin mtight">
                    ∩
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
                    B
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    ∣
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​

              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.52em;">
                <span class="">

           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.53em; vertical-align: -0.52em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
            </span>
            <span class="mfrac">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.01em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.655em;">
