     <li>
      <p>
       Euclidean Distance:
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          d 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           p 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           q 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           = 
          
          
           
           
             ( 
            
            
            
              p 
             
            
              1 
             
            
           
             − 
            
            
            
              q 
             
            
              1 
             
            
            
            
              ) 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             + 
            
           
             ( 
            
            
            
              p 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             − 
            
            
            
              q 
             
            
              2 
             
            
            
            
              ) 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             + 
            
           
             ⋯ 
            
           
             + 
            
           
             ( 
            
            
            
              p 
             
            
              n 
             
            
           
             − 
            
            
            
              q 
             
            
              n 
             
            
            
            
              ) 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
          
         
        
          d(\bold{p},\bold{q})=\sqrt{(p_1-q_1)^2+(p_2-q_2)^2+\cdots+(p_n-q_n)^2}
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            d
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathbf">
            p
           </span>
           <span class="mpunct">
            ,
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathbf">
            q
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            =
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.24em; vertical-align: -0.305em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord sqrt">
            <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
             <span class="vlist-r">
              <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.935em;">
               <span class="svg-align" style="top: -3.2em;">
                <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.2em;">
                </span>
                <span class="mord" style="padding-left: 1em;">
                 <span class="mopen">
                  (
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal">
                   p
                  </span>
                  <span class="msupsub">
                   <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
                      <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                       <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                       </span>
                       <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                        <span class="mord mtight">
                         1
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                     <span class="vlist-s">
                      ​
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                      <span class="">
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="mbin">
                  −
                 </span>
                 <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                   q
                  </span>
                  <span class="msupsub">
                   <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
                      <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                       <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                       </span>
                       <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                        <span class="mord mtight">
                         1
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                     <span class="vlist-s">
                      ​
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                      <span class="">
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span class="mclose">
                  <span class="mclose">
                   )
                  </span>

                      <span class="vlist-r">

                         <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">

               </span>

              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8296em;">
                <span class="">

               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="mclose nulldelimiter">
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       with USE
      </p>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     实验发现：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       这个模型效果比较好，速度也快
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       长文本的攻击效果弱于短文本
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       评分上：逆转负面评价到正面评价会部分失败
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       数据集上负面词多于正面词
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       扰动类型的影响：字符级替代最难被发现造成词表之外的现象
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/2f75a577e3c240eab6bc1d3c719912ed.png"/>
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="Toxic_Content_Detection_365">
     </a>
     Toxic Content Detection
    </h5>
    <p>
     数据集：Kaggle Toxic Comment Classification competation
    </p>
    <p>
     受害模型：LR, CNN, LSTM
    </p>
    <p>
     实验结果：
    </p>
    <p>
     <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/4581d277f48941949a208bcb91a83057.png"/>
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="Potential_Defenses_374">
     </a>
     Potential Defenses
    </h4>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       Spelling Check
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Adversarial Training
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h3>
     <a id="Generating_Natural_Language_Adversarial_Examples_through_Probability_Weighted_Word_Saliency_380">
     </a>
     Generating Natural Language Adversarial Examples through Probability Weighted Word Saliency
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      作者：Shuhuai Ren, Yihe Deng et al.
     </p>
     <p>
      单位：杭州科技大学、加利福尼亚大学、哈工大
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="Introduction_386">
     </a>
     Introduction
    </h4>
    <p>
     NLP对抗样本难的问题：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       words in sentences are discrete tokens
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       hard in human’s perception to make sense of the texts with perturbations
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     本文的出发点：could guarantee the lexical correctness with little grammatical error and semantic shifting.
    </p>
    <p>
     提出的方法：Probability Weighted Word Saliency (PWWS)
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="Text_Classification_Attack_398">
     </a>
     Text Classification Attack
    </h4>
    <p>
     特征空间
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        X 
        
       
      
        X
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">

        </span>

      </span>
     </span>
     ，输出空间
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">

    <h5>
     <a id="Text_Adversarial_Example_402">
     </a>
     Text Adversarial Example
    </h5>
    <p>
     模型分类：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        arg max 
          
         
           ⁡ 
          
         
         
          
          
            y 
           
          
            i 
           
          
         
           ∈ 
          
         
           Y 
          
         
        
       
         ( 
        
        
        
          y 
         
        
          i 
         
        
       
         ∣ 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          y 
         
         
         
           t 
          
         
           r 
          
         
           u 
          
         
           e 
          
         
        
       
      
        \argmax\limits_{y_i\in Y}(y_i|x)=y_{true}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.8249em; vertical-align: -1.0749em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mop op-limits">
          <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
           <span class="vlist-r">
            <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.4306em;">
             <span class="" style="top: -2.1612em; margin-left: 0em;">
              <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
              </span>
              <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
               <span class="mord mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                  y
                 </span>
                 <span class="msupsub">
                  <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                   <span class="vlist-r">
                    <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3281em;">
                     <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                      <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                      </span>
                      <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                       <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                        i
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span class="vlist-s">
                     ​
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span class="vlist-r">
                    <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;">
                     <span class="">
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="mrel mtight">
                 ∈
                </span>
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
                 Y
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="" style="top: -3em;">
              <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
              </span>
              <span class="">
               <span class="mop">
                <span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.0139em;">
                 arg

                <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
                </span>
                <span class="mord mathrm">
                 max
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-s">
             ​

          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
           y
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

         </span>

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">

            <span class="vlist-r">

               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">

                 </span>

                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">

              </span>
             </span>

          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     扰动

     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        p

     范数为：

           1

    <p>
     该论文中，通过替代输入单词的同义词（来自WordNet）并通过取代相似的命名实体(Name Entries, NE)以生成对抗样本
    </p>

    <h5>
     <a id="PWWWS_418">
     </a>
     PWWWS
    </h5>
    <p>
     PWWS属于贪心算法
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      单词替代策略
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       对于单词
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          w 
           
          
            i 
           
          
         
           ∈ 
          
         
           x 
          
         
        
          w_i\in x
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6891em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
             w
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                   i
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            ∈
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            x
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       ，首先用WordNet构建同义词集
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          L 
           
          
            i 
           
          
         
           ⊆ 
          
         
           D 
          
         
        
          \mathbb{L}_i\subseteq \mathbb{D}
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8389em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathbb">
             L
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">

       替代词选择策略：

      <ul>
       <li>
        <p>
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">

               arg max

                w

            w^*_i=R(w_i,\mathbb{L}_i)=\argmax_{w'_i\in \mathbb{L}_i}{P(y_{true}|x'_i)}

               </span>
               <span class="msupsub">
                <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                 <span class="vlist-r">
                  <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7519em;">
                   <span class="" style="top: -2.4413em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

                    <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                     <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                      i
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                    <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

                    <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                     <span class="mord mtight">

                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span class="vlist-s">

                  </span>
                 </span>

              <span class="mclose">

              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         ，其中
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            x 
            
           
             = 
            
            
            
              w 
             
            
              1 
             
            
            
            
              w 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             ⋯ 
            
            
            
              w 
             
            
              i 
             
            
           
             ⋯ 
            
            
            
              w 
             
            
              n 
             
            
           
          
            x=w_1 w_2\cdots w_i\cdots w_n
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">

             <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
              P
             </span>
             <span class="mopen">
              (
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
               y
              </span>
              <span class="msupsub">
               <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2806em;">
                  <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                   </span>
                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mtight">
                     <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                      t
                     </span>
                     <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
                      r
                     </span>
                     <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                      u
                     </span>
                     <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">

                     </span>

              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              ∣
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              <span class="mord mathnormal">
               x
              </span>
              <span class="msupsub">
               <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6887em;">
                  <span class="" style="top: -2.4413em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                     i
                    </span>
                   </span>

                  <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

                    <span class="mbin mtight">
                     ∗
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span class="vlist-s">

                <span class="vlist-r">

             <span class="mclose">

             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </p>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     <strong>
      替换顺序策略
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <p>
     进行切片打分，切片打分函数为：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        S 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          w 
         
        
          i 
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         =

         ( 
        
        
        
          y

           r 
          
         
           u 
          
         
           e 
          
         
        
       
         ∣ 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         − 
        
       
         P 
        
       
         (

         ∣ 
        
        
         
         
           x 
          
         
           i 
          
         
        
          ^ 
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        S(x,w_i)=P(y_{true}|x)-P(y_{true}|\hat{x_i})

    <p>
     对所有
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        w 
         
        
          i 
         
        
       
         ∈ 
        
       
         x 
        
       
      
        w_i\in x
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6891em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
           w

         <span class="mord mathnormal">

      </span>
     </span>
     计算切片分数，获得最佳切片向量

    <h3>
     <a id="Wordlevel_Textual_Adversarial_Attacking_as_Combinatorial_Optimization_441">
     </a>
     Word-level Textual Adversarial Attacking as Combinatorial Optimization
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      作者：Yuan Zang, Fanchao Qi et al.
     </p>
     <p>
      单位：清华大学
     </p>
     <p>
      来源：ACL 2020
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="Introduction_450">
     </a>
     Introduction
    </h4>
    <p>
     基本点：把对抗那个样本攻击当作是组合优化问题
    </p>
    <p>
     方法：基于义元(sememe)的单词替代方法 + 基于粒子群优化的搜索算法
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="Background_456">
     </a>
     Background
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      Sememes
     </strong>
     : 义元是单词的语义标签，相关工作有HowNet
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      PSO
     </strong>
     : 连续空间
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">

         ∈ 
        
        
        
          R

       初始化，随机初始化每个粒子的位置和速度，初始速度的维度为

             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    ma
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    x
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            ]
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       记录，搜索空间的每个位置对应于一个优化分数，最高优化分数记录为个体最佳位置。个体最佳位置中的最高分数为全局最佳位置
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       终止，如果全局最佳位置已经达到期待的最佳分数，则算法终止
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       更新，未终止则更新速度与位置，更新的公式为：
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          v 
           
          
            d 
           
          
            n 
           
          
         
           = 
          
         
           w 
          
          
          
            v 
           
          
            d 
           
          
            n 
           
          
         
           + 
          
          
          
            c 
           
          
            1 
           
          
         
           × 
          
          
          
            r 
           
          
            1 
           
          
         
           × 
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            p 
           
          
            d 
           
          
            n 
           
          
         
           − 
          
          
          
            x 
           
          
            d 
           
          
            n 
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           + 
          
          
          
            c 
           
          
            2 
           
          
         
           × 
          
          
          
            r 
           
          
            2 
           
          
         
           × 
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            p 
           
          
            d 
           
          
            g 
           
          
         
           − 
          
          
          
            x 
           
          
            d 
           
          
            n 
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          v^n_d=wv^n_d+c_1\times r_1\times (p^n_d - x^n_d) + c_2 \times r_2 \times (p^g_d-x^n_d)
         </span>

             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">

                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">

                  </span>

               </span>

               </span>
              </span>

             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       ，其中
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          w 
          
         
        
          w
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
            w
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       是惯性权重，
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">

       个粒子的个体最佳位置与全局最佳位置，

    <h4>
     <a id="Methodology_470">
     </a>
     Methodology
    </h4>
    <p>
     two parts: sememe-based word substitution &amp; PSO-based adversarial example search
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="Sememebased_Word_Substitution_474">
     </a>
     Sememe-based Word Substitution
    </h5>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       只替代content words (words that carry meanings and consist mostly of nouns, verbs, adjectives and adverbs)，并限制替代词跟原单词part-of-speech tag相同
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          w 
           
          
            ∗ 
           
          
         
        
          w^*
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6887em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
             w
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6887em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mbin mtight">
                   ∗
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       替代
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          w 
          
         
        
          w
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
            w
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       时，当且仅当
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          w 
          
         
        
          w
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
            w
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       的意义跟
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          w 
           
          
            ∗ 
           
          
         
        
          w_*
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.5806em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
             w
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1757em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mbin mtight">
                   ∗
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       的意义有相同的义元
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h5>
     <a id="PSObased_adversarial_example_search_480">
     </a>
     PSO-based adversarial example search
    </h5>
    <p>
     一个位置对应于一个句子，每个位置的维度对应于句子的每个单词
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          w 
         
        
          1 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         ⋯ 
        
        
        
          w 
         
        
          d 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         ⋯ 
        
        
        
          w 
         
        
          D 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          w 
         
        
          d 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         ∈ 
        
       
         V 
        
       
         ( 
        
        
        
          w 
         
        
          d 
         
        
          o 
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        x^n=w^n_1 \cdots w^n_d \cdots w^n_D, w^n_d\in \mathbb{V}(w^o_d)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6644em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9475em; vertical-align: -0.2831em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">

          ⋯
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0331em; vertical-align: -0.2831em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathbb">
          V
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
           w
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.4169em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 d
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">

         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        V 
        
       
         ( 
        
        
        
          w 
         
        
          d 
         
        
          o 
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        \mathbb{V}(w^o_d)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0331em; vertical-align: -0.2831em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathbb">
          V
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
           w
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.4169em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 d
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">

             </span>

             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2831em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     包含了
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        w 
         
        
          d 
         
        
          o 
         
        
       
      
        w^o_d
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9475em; vertical-align: -0.2831em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
           w
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.4169em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 d
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 o
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">

             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2831em;">

              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     与其替代词，
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        D 
        
       
      
        D
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
          D
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     为原始输入的长度
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      初始化
     </strong>
     ：随机替换原始输入的一个词以决定粒子的初始化位置
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      记录
     </strong>
     ：与原PSO算法相同
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      终止
     </strong>
     ：受害模型预测到攻击者期待得到的结果标签
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      更新
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>

     <li>
      <p>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          w 
          
         
        
          w
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
            w
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       是惯性系数，
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          I 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           a 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           b 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          I(a,b)
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
            I
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            a
           </span>
           <span class="mpunct">
            ,
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            b
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       定义为：
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          I 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           a 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           b 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           = 
          
          
          
            { 
           
           
            
             
              
               
               
                 1 
                
               
                 , 
                
               
              
             
             
              
               
               
                 a 
                
               
                 = 
                
               
                 b 
                
               
              
             
            
            
             
              
               
               
                 − 
                
               
                 1 
                
               
                 , 
                
               
              
             
             
              
               
               
                 a 
                
               
                 ≠ 
                
               
                 b 
                
               
              
             
            
           
          
         
        
          I(a,b)=\begin{cases}1,&amp;a=b\\ -1,&amp;a\not=b\end{cases}
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
            I
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            a
           </span>
           <span class="mpunct">
            ,
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            b
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            =
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 3em; vertical-align: -1.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="minner">
            <span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">
             <span class="delimsizing size4">
              {
              <!-- -->
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="mord">
             <span class="mtable">
              <span class="col-align-l">

      <ul>
       <li>
        <p>
         第一步，新的移动概率
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            P 
             
            
              i 
             
            
           
          
            P_i
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
               P
              </span>
              <span class="msupsub">
               <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
                  <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                   </span>
                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                     i
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span class="vlist-s">
                  ​
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                  <span class="">
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         随粒子被引入到个体最佳位置，当粒子决定移动时，位置的每个维度由相同维度的速度决定，通过
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            s 
            
           
             i 
            
           
             g 
            
           
             m 
            
           
             o 
            
           
             i 
            
           
             d 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             ⋅ 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
            sigmoid(\cdot)
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal">
              s
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal">
              i
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
              g
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal">
              m
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal">
              o
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal">
              i
             </span>
             <span class="mord mathnormal">
              d
             </span>
             <span class="mopen">
              (
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              ⋅
             </span>
             <span class="mclose">
              )
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         函数进行概率评判。其中
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            P 
             
            
              i 
             
            
           
          
            P_i
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
               P
              </span>
              <span class="msupsub">
               <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
                  <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

         为：
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">

            P 
             
            
              i

               a 
              
             
               x 
              
             
            
           
             −

               m 
              
             
               a

             − 
            
            
            
              P 
             
             
             
               m 
              
             
               i 
              
             
               n 
              
             
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
            P_i=P_{max}-\frac{t}{T}\times (P_{max}-P_{min})
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">

             <span class="mrel">

             </span>
             <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="base">

              <span class="msupsub">

                <span class="vlist-r">

                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mtight">

                     </span>

                     </span>

              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">

             <span class="mbin">

             </span>
             <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="base">

             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
              </span>
              <span class="mfrac">
               <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                <span class="vlist-r">

                  <span class="" style="top: -3.23em;">

       更新后应用突变：

                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="mclose nulldelimiter">
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       ，
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          ϵ 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           ⋅ 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          \epsilon(\cdot)
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            ϵ
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            ⋅
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       为编辑距离。之后，返回记录步骤
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h4>
     <a id="Experiments_508">
     </a>
     Experiments
    </h4>
    <p>
     数据集：IMDB、SST-2、NLI、SNLI
    </p>
    <p>
     baseline：Embedding/LM + Genetic、SYNONYM + Greedy
    </p>
    <p>
     Evaluation Metrics:
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       Attack Success Rate (ASR)
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Attack Validity
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       Quality of adversarial examples (modification rate, grammatical error increase rate, language model perplexity)
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h3>
     <a id="Contextualized_Perturbation_for_Textual_Adversarial_Attack_522">
     </a>
     Contextualized Perturbation for Textual Adversarial Attack
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      作者：Dianqi Li, Yizhe Zhang et al.
     </p>
     <p>
      单位：华盛顿大学、微软研究院、杜克大学
     </p>
     <p>
      来源：NAACL 2021
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="Introduction_531">
     </a>
     Introduction
    </h4>
    <p>
     Problem: rule-based methods are agnostic to context, limiting their ability to produce natural, fluent, and grammatical outputs
    </p>
    <p>
     ContextuaLized AdversaRial Example: CLARE, a mask-then-infill procedure
    </p>
    <p>
     CLARE features three contextualized perturbations: Replace, Insert and Merge
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="CLARE_539">
     </a>
     CLARE
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="Background_541">
     </a>

    <h5>
     <a id="Masking_and_Contextualized_Infilling_549">
     </a>
     Masking and Contextualized Infilling
    </h5>
    <p>
     <strong>
      Replace
     </strong>
     :
    </p>
    <p>
     对于给定的第
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        i 
        
       
      
        i
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">

          i
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     个位置，首先给
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
         
        
          i 
         
        
       
      
        x_i
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">

           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">

    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
          
         
           ~ 
          
         
        
          z 
         
        
       
         = 
        
       
         r 
        
       
         e 
        
       
         p 
        
       
         l 
        
       
         a 
        
       
         c 
        
       
         e 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         , 
        
       
         i 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          1 
         
        
       
         ⋯ 
        
        
        
          x 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           − 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
         z 
        
        
        
          x 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           + 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
         ⋯ 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        \tilde{x}_z = replace(x,i)=x_1\cdots x_{i-1}z x_{i+1}\cdots x_n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">

                           <span class="mord mtight">
                            ′
                           </span>
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            &gt;
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0197em;">
            l
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            }
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       ，
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          V 
          
         
        
          V
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">

           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
            V
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       为语言建模模型的单词表，从
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">

         </span>

           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       中挑选token填充
      </p>
     </li>

    <p>
     <strong>
      Merge
     </strong>
     : 就是二元词组换成一元词
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
         
        
          ~ 
         
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          1 
         
        
       
         ⋯ 
        
        
        
          x 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           − 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
         [ 
        
       
         M 
        
       
         A 
        
       
         S 
        
       
         K 
        
       
         ] 
        
        
        
          x 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           + 
          
         
           2 
          
         
        
       
         ⋯ 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        \tilde{x}=x_1\cdots x_{i-1} [MASK] x_{i+2} \cdots x_n
       </span>

    </p>
    <p>
     对于输入序列每个位置，CLARE进行替换或插入或合并，之后通过语言建模模型和文本相似度函数构建候选令牌集，最小化正确标签的概率的令牌当作替代令牌。
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="Sequentially_Applying_the_PErturbations_589">
     </a>
     Sequentially Applying the PErturbations
    </h4>
    <p>
     输入对：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         , 
        
       
         y 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        (x,y)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
          y
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
        
       
      
        x
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的长度为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        n 
        
       
      
        n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，若候选集不为空，共进行
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        3 
        
       
         n 
        
       
      
        3n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          3
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     个操作，操作为那三种，所有操作的应用操作表示为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        a 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        a(x)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          a
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     。
    </p>
    <p>
     每一步都计算一个评分：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        s 
         
         
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           y 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         a 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         − 
        
        
        
          p 
         
        
          f 
         
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         y 
        
       
         ∣ 
        
       
         a 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        s_{(x,y)}(a)=-p_f(y|a(x))
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.1052em; vertical-align: -0.3552em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           s
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mopen mtight">
                  (
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  x
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">

                 </span>
                 <span class="mclose mtight">
                  )
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3552em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>

           </span>

          (
         </span>

         </span>
         <span class="mclose">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0361em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          −
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           p
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">

                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">

             </span>
            </span>

              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
          y
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          ∣
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          a
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">

         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>

    <p>
     每个位置只有一种操作被应用到。

    <h3>
     <a id="FrequencyGuided_Word_Substitutions_for_Detecting_Textual_Adversarial_Examples_600">
     </a>
     Frequency-Guided Word Substitutions for Detecting Textual Adversarial Examples
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      作者：Xinghao Yang, Yongshun Gong et al.
     </p>
     <p>
      单位：IEEE
     </p>
     <p>
      来源：Trans on Cybernetics
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="Algorithm_609">
     </a>
     Algorithm
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="Black_Box_settings_611">
     </a>
     Black Box settings
    </h5>
    <p>
     提供的：输入文本
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
        
       
         ∈ 
        
       
         X 
        
       
      
        x\in X
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.5782em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          ∈
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
          X
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，DNN模型
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        F 
        
       
      
        F
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">
          F
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，正确标签
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        y 
         
         
         
           t 
          
         
           r 
          
         
           u 
          
         
           e 
          
         
        
       
         ∈ 
        
       
         Y 
        
       
      
        y_{true}\in Y
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7335em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
           y
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2806em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  t
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">

                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">

                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">

                </span>

              </span>

             </span>

              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          ∈
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
          Y
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，i.e.,
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">

        F(x)=y_{true}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">

         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          x
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">

         <span class="mrel">

         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
           y
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2806em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

    <h5>
     <a id="Sementic_Similarity_615">
     </a>
     Sementic Similarity
    </h5>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        E 
        
       
         n 
        
       
         c 
        
       
         o 
        
       
         d 
        
       
         e 
        
       
         r 
        
       
      
        Encoder
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          E
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          co
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          d
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
          er
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        U 
        
       
         S 
        
       
         E 
        
       
      
        USE
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">
          U
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          SE
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的编码器
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        U 
        
       
         S 
        
        
        
          E 
         
         
         
           s 
          
         
           c 
          
         
           o 
          
         
           r

         = 
        
       
         C 
        
       
         o 
        
       
         s 
        
       
         i 
        
       
         n 
        
       
         e 
        
       
         (

         e

         (

        USE_{score}=Cosine(Encoder(x),Encoder(x_{adv}))
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">
          U
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          S
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
           E
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0576em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  score
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
          C
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          os
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          in
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          e
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">

         </span>

         <span class="mpunct">
