    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="Bigram__Unigram_Candidate_Selection_621">
     </a>
     Bigram &amp; Unigram Candidate Selection
    </h5>
    <p>
     使用WordNet (Synonym来源，假定WordNet的同义词空间为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        W 
        
       
      
        \mathbb{W}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6889em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathbb">
          W
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ) 跟HowNet (sememes，假定义元空间为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        H 
        
       
      
        \mathbb{H}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6889em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathbb">
          H
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     )。
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       创建候选集，
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <p>

         若

     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       选择最佳候选：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <p>
         对于候选集
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            S 
             
            
              i 
             
            
           
          
            S_i
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
               S
              </span>
              <span class="msupsub">
               <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
                  <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0576em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                   </span>
                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                     i
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span class="vlist-s">
                  ​
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
                  <span class="">
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         ，候选重要性分数为：
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            I 
             
             
             
               w 
              
             
               i 
              
             
               ′ 
              
             
            
           
             = 
            
           
             P 
            
           
             ( 
            
            
            
              y 
             
             
             
               t 
              
             
               r 
              
             
               u 
              
             
               e 
              
             
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
             − 
            
           
             P 
            
           
             ( 
            
            
            
              y 
             
             
             
               t 
              
             
               r 
              
             
               u 
              
             
               e 
              
             
            
           
             ∣ 
            
            
            
              x 
             
            
              i 
             
            
              ′ 
             
            
           
             ) 
            
           
             , 
            
           
             ∀ 
            
            
            
              w 
             
            
              i 
             
            
              ′ 
             
            
           
             ∈ 
            
            
            
              S 
             
            
              i 
             
            
           
          
            I_{w'_i}=P(y_{true}|x)-P(y_{true}|x'_i), \forall w'_i\in \mathbb{S}_i
           </span>
           <span class="katex-html">
            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0833em; vertical-align: -0.3999em;">
             </span>
             <span class="mord">
              <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">
               I
              </span>
              <span class="msupsub">
               <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;">
                  <span class="" style="top: -2.5257em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                   </span>
                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mtight">
                     <span class="mord mtight">
                      <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
                       w
                      </span>
                      <span class="msupsub">
                       <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                        <span class="vlist-r">
                         <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7416em;">
                          <span class="" style="top: -2.1777em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                           <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                           </span>
                           <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                            <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                             i

        <p>
         最佳候选：
         <span class="katex--inline">
          <span class="katex">
           <span class="katex-mathml">
            w 
             
            
              i 
             
            
              ∗ 
             
            
           
             = 
            
           
             R

                w

               i 
              
             
               ′ 
              
             
            
           
          
            w^*_i=R(w_i,\mathbb{S}_i)=\argmax\limits_{w'_i\in \mathbb{S}_i} I_{

            {w}'_i}
           </span>

            <span class="base">
             <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9474em; vertical-align: -0.2587em;">

             <span class="mord">
              <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
               w
              </span>
              <span class="msupsub">
               <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                <span class="vlist-r">
                 <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6887em;">
                  <span class="" style="top: -2.4413em; margin-left: -0.0269em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                   </span>
                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                    <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                     i
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                  <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                   <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                   </span>
                   <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">

    <h5>
     <a id="Semantic_Preservation_Optimization_637">
     </a>
     Semantic Preservation Optimization
    </h5>
    <p>
     SPO用于优化单词替代顺序优先级，通过三个目标：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <p>
       成功攻击
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       最小替代
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       语义不变
      </p>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     获得的
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        n 
        
       
      
        n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     个对抗语句：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        { 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          1 
         
        
          ∗ 
         
        
       
         , 
        
       
         ⋯ 
         
       
         , 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          n 
         
        
          ∗ 
         
        
       
         } 
        
       
      
        \{x^*_1,\cdots, x^*_n\}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          {
          <!-- -->
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6887em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.4519em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 1
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="minner">
          ⋯
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">

         <span class="mpunct">

                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mbin mtight">
                 ∗
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.247em;">

      </span>

     ，从
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        X

       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>

         </span>
        </span>

      </span>
     </span>
     到
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">

       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">

          <span class="msupsub">

            <span class="vlist-r">

               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 i
                </span>
               </span>

              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">

     的差为最大攻击效果：
     <span class="katex--inline">

         x 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         − 
        
       
         P 
        
       
         ( 
        
        
        
          y 
         
         
         
           t 
          
         
           r 
          
         
           u 
          
         
           e 
          
         
        
       
         ∣ 
        
        
        
          x 
         
        
          i 
         
        
          ∗ 
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
      
        \triangle P^*_i=P(y_{true}|x)-P(y_{true}|x^*_i)
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">

         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，直接使用将可能导致替换陷入局部最优而非全局最优。
    </p>
    <p>
     初始的迭代输入：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        G 
         
        
          0 
         
        
       
      
        \mathbb{G}^0
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8141em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathbb">
           G
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8141em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 0
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     阈值：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        M 
        
       
      
        M
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">
          M
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，限制单词被修改的数量
    </p>

     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/136cc4ed206546d2bdbaebcfc933f5b4.png"/>
     <br/>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/e608cfd9b24a4da69dc0962089f00df6.png"/>
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="SPO_with_Semantic_Filter_SPOF_657">
     </a>
     SPO with Semantic Filter (SPOF)
    </h5>
    <p>
     收集可能的对抗样本的空集：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        S 
        
       
         u 
        
       
         c 
        
       
         A 
        
       
         d 
        
       
         v 
        
       
      
        SucAdv
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
          S
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          u
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          A
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          d
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
          v
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/77328852db8849ae929167f8e62b6705.png"/>

    <h4>
     <a id="Experiment_676">
     </a>
     Experiment
    </h4>
    <p>
     数据集：IMDB, AG’s News, Yahoo! Answers
    </p>
    <p>
     受害模型：CNN、Ch-CNN、LSTM、Bi-LSTM
    </p>
    <p>
     评估指标：
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
         S

                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7633em;">

                       <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                       </span>
                       <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                        <span class="mbin mtight">
                         ∗
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                 <span class="mclose mtight">
                  }
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.5896em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="mclose nulldelimiter">
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="Universal_Adversarial_Triggers_for_Attacking_and_Analyzing_NLP_684">
     </a>
     Universal Adversarial Triggers for Attacking and Analyzing NLP
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      作者：Eric Wallace, Shi Feng et al.
     </p>
     <p>
      单位：Allen Institute for AI et al.
     </p>
     <p>
      来源：ACL 2021
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="Abstract__Intro_693">
     </a>
     Abstract &amp; Intro
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      universal adversarial triggers
     </strong>
     : input-agnostic sequences of tokens that trigger a model to produce a specific prediction when concatenated to any input from a dataset.
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      contribution
     </strong>
     : gradient-guided search over tokens which finds short trigger sequences that successfully trigger the target prediction
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      constraint
     </strong>
     : white-box attack to specific model (however, can transfer to other models)
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      triggers
     </strong>
     : a new form of universal adversarial perturbation adapted to discrete textual inputs.
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      finding
     </strong>
     :
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      short sequences can trigger successfully.
     </li>
     <li>
      trigger can be used in transfer learning.
     </li>
     <li>
      identify heuristics learned by SQuAD models
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h4>
     <a id="Universal_Adversarial_Triggers_709">
     </a>
     Universal Adversarial Triggers
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="Setting_and_Motivation_711">
     </a>
     Setting and Motivation
    </h5>
    <p>
     universal adversarial attack:
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      using the exact same attack for any input (Moosavi-Dezfooli 2017, Brown 2017)
     </li>
     <li>
      advantageous: no access to the target model at test time, trigger sequences can be widely distributed for anyone to fool machine learning models.
     </li>
     <li>
      transfer across models and don’t need white-box access to the target model (Moosavi-Dezfooli 2017)
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h5>
     <a id="Attack_Model_and_Objective_719">

    <h5>
     <a id="Trigger_Search_Algorithm_733">
     </a>
     Trigger Search Algorithm
    </h5>
    <p>
     Token Replacement Strategy: based on a linear approximation of the task loss.
    </p>
    <p>
     update the embedding for
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        e 
         
         
         
           a 
          
         
           d 
          
          
          
            v 
           
          
            i 
           
          
         
        
       
      
        e_{adv_i}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6807em; vertical-align: -0.2501em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           e
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  a
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  d
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                   v
                  </span>
                  <span class="msupsub">
                   <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3281em;">
                      <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                       <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                       </span>
                       <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                        <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                         i
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                     <span class="vlist-s">
                      ​
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span class="vlist-r">
                     <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;">
                      <span class="">
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2501em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     to minimize the loss:
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        arg 
          
         
           ⁡ 
          
         
         
          
          
            e 
           
          
            i 
           
          
            ′ 
           
          
         
           ∈ 
          
         
           V 
          
         
        
       
         min 
        
       
         ⁡ 
        
       
         [ 
        
        
        
          e 
         
        
          i 
         
        
          ′ 
         
        
       
         − 
        
        
        
          e 
         
         
         
           a 
          
         
           d 
          
          
          
            v 
           
          
            i 
           
          
         
        
        
        
          ] 
         
        
          ⊤ 
         
        
        
        
          ∇ 
         
         
         
           e 
          
          
          
            a 
           
          
            d 
           
           
           
             v 
            
           
             i 
            
           
          
         
        
       
         L 
        
       
      
        \arg\limits_{e'_i\in V} \min [e'_i-e_{adv_i}]^\top \nabla_{e_{adv_i}} L
       </span>

     </span>
     : computed in brute-force with |V|d dimensional dot products, d is the dimensionality of the token embedding.
    </p>
    <p>
     Process Pic: 先算任务梯度 -&gt; 遍历所有的token取极小 -&gt; 获得极小的token -&gt; 作为trigger结合语句计算概率分布 -&gt; 继续重复以上步骤 -&gt; 目标函数极小得到结果
    </p>
    <p>
     augment: beam search, top-k token considered
    </p>
    <p>
     <img alt="外链图片转存失败,源站可能有防盗链机制,建议将图片保存下来直接上传" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/af2bcb1a077b4dba811b5785c6dcfd4d.jpeg"/>
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="Tasks_and_Associated_Loss_Functions_752">
     </a>
     Tasks and Associated Loss Functions
    </h5>
    <p>
     Classification: bypass fake news detection by trigger.
    </p>
    <p>
     Reading Comprehension: modify a web page in order to trigger malicious or vulgar answers, focus on why, who, when and where questions.
    </p>
    <p>
     Conditional Text Generation: create triggers that are prepended before t to let model generate similar content to a set of targets Y. Maximize the likelihood of racist outputs by minimizing the following loss:
     <br/>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">

    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="Attacking_Text_Classification_761">
     </a>
     Attacking Text Classification
    </h4>
    <p>
     two text classification datasets.
    </p>
    <p>
     Sentiment Analysis: Stanford Sentiment Treebank, Bi-LSTM model, word2vec / ELMo embeddings.
    </p>
    <p>
     Natural Language Inference: SNLI dataset, ESIM, DA-GloVe, DA-ELMo.
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="Breaking_Sentiment_Analysis_769">
     </a>
     Breaking Sentiment Analysis
    </h5>
    <p>
     pre-avoid: use a lexicon to blacklist sentiment words. “zoning tapping fiennes” is a trigger.
    </p>
    <p>
     ELMo-based Model: “uˆ{b”, “m&amp;s~” are triggers, droping accuracy.
    </p>
    <h5>
     <a id="Breaking_Natural_Language_Inference_775">
     </a>
     Breaking Natural Language Inference
    </h5>
    <p>
     motivation: threat the accuracy.
    </p>
    <p>
     attack SNLI models, result is here: these trigger can degrade the three model’s accuracy to nearly 0.
    </p>
    <p>
     the attack also readily transfer.
    </p>
    <p>
     <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/28c1fe7360334ccfa22db25ab2bf29eb.jpeg"/>
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="Attacking_Reading_Comprehension_786">
     </a>
     Attacking Reading Comprehension
    </h4>
    <p>
     motivation: answer the specific answer just like a backdoor to trigger
    </p>
    <p>
     triggers for SQuAD: use an simple baseline and test the trigger’s transferability to more advanced models
    </p>
    <p>
     embedding: GloVe
    </p>
    <p>
     target answer: ‘to kill anmerican people’、‘donald trump’、‘january 2014’、‘new york’
    </p>
    <p>
     question type: why, who, when, where.
    </p>
    <p>
     Results:
     <img alt="" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/bab51261c959467b970ab3a7a866917f.jpeg"/>
    </p>
    <p>
     transferability:
    </p>
    <p>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/direct/27f251985bf845cd8237a58ad34d4ee4.jpeg"/>
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="Analyzing_The_Trigger_806">
     </a>
     Analyzing The Trigger
    </h4>
    <p>
     Triggers Align With SNLI Artifacts:
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      dataset artifacts are successful triggers，‘no’、‘tv’、‘naked’ can drop accuracy.
     </li>
     <li>
      entailment overlap bias
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     explain the triggers:
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      PMI Analysis: question-correlation answer triggers have high PMI values,
      <span class="katex--inline">
       <span class="katex">

     <li>
      Question Type Matching
     </li>
     <li>
      token order, Placement, and Removal: model is sensitive to token order, trigger is not very correlated with replacement, remove tokens can increase the success rate when transferring the triggers to black-box models.
